 in chaatro ke samarthan main yahaan ke resident doctor bhi hadtaal par chale gaye hai

 police ne jabaran opidi khulwaane kii koshish kii to hadataali doctoron ke saath uski jhadap ho gai

 ye thik ho jayega, wo thik ho jayega
 v backers are new organizations, old unions
 donon kii maang main antar he
 The old union wants that the union and the Indian Bank Association should decide the salary according to the banks
 ve bankers kaa kahana he ki ham sarkari bank hai to ham sarkari karmchaaree kyon nahin hai

 ve bankers kaa kahana he ki is ek antar ke alaava unase alag nahin hai
 The demand of v bankers states that those demands can be raised even by wearing black T-shirt whose IT cell can call you communist
 aap rang badal len magar theke kii naukari karne vaale hazaron log milte hai jo tut chuke hai
 They have nothing left
 isliye ye nai pension niti kaa virodh kar rahe hai
 People of other professions are also doing it
 magar koi mil kar nahin lard rahaa, sab pension ke sawaal par alag alag lard rahe hai
 Railway union people also came to Jantar Mantar last week, they were also opposing the new pension policy
 jantar-mantar par ye noujvaan banker apane liye nahin, balki berojgaar bharat ke liye bhi ladane aae the
 They say that there is a lot of vacancy in banks
 ek aadmi teen se chaar aadmi kaa kaam kar rahaa he

 gramin bank se ritair hue logon kaa haal bahut bura he

 ritair kar chuke hai magar pension mil rahaa he 1800

 buudhvaar ke pradarshan main desh bhar ke gramin bank ke afasar karmchaaree shaamil hue

 hamane pichhali baar dikhaaya tha ki kaise aadesh aata he ki biimaar padane par zile se baahar nahin janaa he ilaaj ke liye
 The language of the order changes after we show it
 magar inaki selary kii bhi bahut samasya he
 Earlier everyone was fighting their own battles but now they are coming together
 kai shakhaon main staff nahin he, ek hi staff ke bharose kaam chal rahaa he

 tippaniyan No one is listening to their ex-servicemen bankers
 jabaki ve to kam se kam deshbhakt honge hi

 jab gangamain aapako patr likhane lage to samaj sakate hai ki aap sahi raste par hai

 hamaari is series kaa asar logon ke zamir par bhi pad rahaa he
 a banker has written that it is pressured that whoever comes to the bank, has to download the Bhima app with his mobile
 bahut log mobile nahin dena chaahate magar unase lekar das bees bhim ap downlod karnaa padataa he varanaa daant padati he

 sabhi upabhoktaaon se paise letaa he

 banker andar ho rahi in gadabadiyon ko dekhakar aahat hai

 mobile phone par gaali dena kam ho rahaa he magar target kaa dabaav kam nahin hua he

 aaj hi udai kotak kaa bayaan padhaa he ki lone ke enpie main ho jane kaa doosraa jaljla laghu madhyam udyogon ke sector se aa rahaa he

 vaise logon ko diya ja rahaa he jo lenaa bhi nahin chaahate or lene ke yogya bhi nahin hai
 We better be cautious first
 jo banker kal tak apana naam or cheharaa chipa kar bol rahe the
 Hidden in some darkness with his torture, today he came into the light wearing the same dark colored T-shirt
 ab aap inhen dekh sakate hai, inkaa naam jaan sakate hai, inhen bolte hue sun sakate hai

 ve bankers nayaa samooh he, zyaadaatar yuva hai
 v bankers believe that their salary should be equal to the central government employees
 jab chairman or kaaryakari nideshak ko saatven vetan ayog ke hisaab se vetan miltaa he to banker ko kyon nahin mil rahaa he
 If this is the case then there is a lot of power in this bade afasar ko kisi or vyavastha ke tahat vetan mili or baakiyon ko vetan itnaa kam mili, isaki vyavastha kar di jaae
 i do not think anyone would accept this argument, at least the Chairman and the Executive Directors should not have taken their salary according to the Seventh Pay Commission because the officers under them do not get salary accordingly
 is samooh main sirf yuva banker nahin hai balki bhootpurv sainik banker bhi hai or badi sankhya main gramin bainkon main kaam karne vaale bhi hai
 Which says that 30,000 people are not even getting pension
 jinhen miltaa he unhen maheene kaa 1800 hi miltaa he

 13 lakh se adhik bankeron kii zindagi main yatnaa ghus gai he

 aap yah na samajhen ki isamen dilli ke banker hai
